# Changelog

## [Unreleased]

### Added
- `Badge` entity class with attributes and annotations.
- Dependencies for Spring Boot Web, JPA, H2 database, jaxb-api, and org.javassist in `pom.xml`.
- H2 database configuration in `application.properties`.
- Hardcoded data for 5 badges in `data.sql`.
- `BadgeRepository` interface extending JpaRepository.
- `BadgeService` class for fetching all badges from the database.
- `BadgeController` REST controller with GET endpoint for badges.## Changelog

- H2 database configuration in `application.properties`.
- Hardcoded data for 5 badges in `data.sql`.
- `BadgeRepository` interface extending JpaRepository.
- `BadgeService` class for fetching all badges from the database.
- `BadgeController` REST controller with GET endpoint for badges. # Changelog

- Dependencies for Spring Boot Web, JPA, H2 database, jaxb-api, and org.javassist in `pom.xml`.
- H2 database configuration in `application.properties`.
- Hardcoded data for 5 badges in `data.sql`.
- `BadgeRepository` interface extending JpaRepository.
- `BadgeService` class for fetching all badges from the database.
- `BadgeController` REST controller with GET endpoint for badges.v# Changelog

- Dependencies for Spring Boot Web, JPA, H2 database, jaxb-api, and org.javassist in `pom.xml`.
- H2 database configuration in `application.properties`.
- Hardcoded data for 5 badges in `data.sql`.
- `BadgeRepository` interface extending JpaRepository.
- `BadgeService` class for fetching all badges from the database.
- `BadgeController` REST controller with GET endpoint for badges.m# Changelog

- Hardcoded data for 5 badges in `data.sql`.
- `BadgeRepository` interface extending JpaRepository.
- `BadgeService` class for fetching all badges from the database.
- `BadgeController` REST controller with GET endpoint for badges.d# Changelog

### Added
- `Badge` entity class with attributes and annotations.
- Dependencies for Spring Boot Web, JPA, H2 database, jaxb-api, and org.javassist in `pom.xml`.
- H2 database configuration in `application.properties`.
- Hardcoded data for 5 badges in `data.sql`.
- `BadgeRepository` interface extending JpaRepository.
- `BadgeService` class for fetching all badges from the database.
- `BadgeController` REST controller with GET endpoint for badges.-# Changelog

- Hardcoded data for 5 badges in `data.sql`.
- `BadgeRepository` interface extending JpaRepository.
- `BadgeService` class for fetching all badges from the database.

- Dependencies for Spring Boot Web, JPA, H2 database, jaxb-api, and org.javassist in `pom.xml`.
- H2 database configuration in `application.properties`.
- Hardcoded data for 5 badges in `data.sql`.
- `BadgeRepository` interface extending JpaRepository.
- `BadgeService` class for fetching all badges from the database.
- `BadgeController` REST controller with GET endpoint for badges.g# Changelog

- Hardcoded data for 5 badges in `data.sql`.
- `BadgeRepository` interface extending JpaRepository.
- `BadgeService` class for fetching all badges from the database.
- `BadgeController` REST controller with GET endpoint for badges.S# Changelog

- Dependencies for Spring Boot Web, JPA, H2 database, jaxb-api, and org.javassist in `pom.xml`.
- H2 database configuration in `application.properties`.
- Hardcoded data for 5 badges in `data.sql`.
- `BadgeRepository` interface extending JpaRepository.
- `BadgeService` class for fetching all badges from the database.
- `BadgeController` REST controller with GET endpoint for badges.r# Changelog
